[2025-11-25T16:22:31Z] Abhishek S: The original Constitution is preserved in one of the world's most sophisticated conservation systems. Two hermetically sealed glass cases filled with nitrogen gas (containing less than 1% oxygen) are installed in the Parliament Library. The cases maintain a constant temperature of 20°C (±2°C) and relative humidity of 40-50%, with humidity at approximately 50 grams per cubic meter to prevent ink oxidation. The internal volume of each case is 96,250 cubic centimeters, with dimensions of 55 cm × 70 cm × 25 cm. These cases are monitored continuously by CCTV, with the gas replaced annually and the system checked every two months. ↵ These cases were built in the X Conservation Institute in the USA and were installed by the institute in 1994. ID X.
